block.U+16800|92160|𖠀..U+16A3F|92735|𖨿

McsHitp-creation:: {2018-09-15},

overview of U+16800..U+16A3F

description::
· Unicode-block-name= Bamum-Supplement
· range= U+16800|92160|𖠀..U+16A3F|92735|𖨿
· plane= plane.1
· quantity-of-code-points= 576
· quantity-of-chars= 569
· script= Bamum
· In the names list, most of the comments are in Latin. Those which have a Luwian phonetic value are identified as syllabic.
[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unicode_character_property#Block]
[ftp://www.unicode.org/Public/UCD/latest/ucd/]
